## Post-roadmap — 2026-07-16 climate resumes on the last holiday day

Traced from the same 12–16 Jul holiday as Batches 132–133. The holiday form labels its
two dates "First day of holiday" / "Last day of holiday" (`HolidayPage.tsx:165`/`:175`),
and Mark travels home on the last day and sleeps in his own bed that night — so the night
of `end_date` is a *home* night, not an away night. Today the bedroom/climate subsystem
gates "away" **end-inclusive** (`active_holiday_window_for_date`, `holiday_pause.py:85`),
so on the last day the Climate tab shows "Holiday away — the room read and fan controls
stay dormant … Climate resumes {endDate}" — a line that already contradicts itself
(`EnvironmentPage.tsx:52`/`:58`) — and the overnight fan autopilot stays a dormant no-op
through the whole 21:30→00:00 pre-sleep slice on the very night he's back, only waking
after midnight once the local date rolls to `end_date+1` (`scheduler.py:1049`, window
`21:30→08:30`, `fan_control.py:46`). So he comes home to a hot room and the fan does
nothing for the first ~2.5 h — exactly the window that matters.

Craig confirmed (2026-07-16) scoping this to the **whole evening / "is he home tonight"
subsystem**, not just the fan: fan control, the bedtime thermal alert, the sleep-protocol
nudge, and the Climate/Tonight UI all resume on `end_date`. The fix is a one-night shift on
the *evening* side only — away nights become `[start, end-1]` (end-exclusive) for those
surfaces. The plan side is deliberately left inclusive: the last day stays a holiday **rest**
(the workout is still `skipped`, `_skip_workouts`), and the morning "last-night" reads —
Sleep's history tab (`SleepPage.tsx:217`) and the brief's thermal review
(`morning_analysis.py`, `insideHolidayWindow`) — correctly stay dormant on `end_date`
morning because they describe the away night just gone. Decision **#211** assigned at
`/batch-start`.

| Batch | Tier | Status | Phases | Goal | Acceptance criteria |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| Batch 134 — Climate/bedroom subsystem resumes on the last holiday day | 🔴 High | Planned | 134.1 Backend "away tonight" semantics — in `holiday_pause.py` add an **end-exclusive** helper `overnight_away_window_for_date(windows, d)` (with a `holiday_windows_away_overnight` mirror of `holiday_windows_covering_date`, and a service method `get_overnight_away_window_for_date`) returning the active window only for `start_date ≤ d < end_date`: Mark returns home the night of `end_date`, so the bedroom/climate subsystem is away only for the nights `[start, end-1]`. Leave the end-inclusive `active_holiday_window_for_date` / `holiday_windows_covering_date` untouched — the plan-rest and morning "last-night" reads still use them.<br>134.2 Evening/overnight scheduler jobs resume on `end_date` — repoint `run_fan_control` (`scheduler.py:1049`), the thermal half of `run_evening_monitoring_alerts` (`scheduler.py:230`), and `run_evening_sleep_nudge` (`scheduler.py:197`) from `get_active_window_for_date` to the end-exclusive `get_overnight_away_window_for_date`, so on the night of `end_date` the overnight fan autopilot reconciles the live room temp, the bedtime thermal check runs, and the sleep-protocol nudge fires — while the last away night (`end_date-1`) stays dormant. No change to fan thresholds, the wind-down, or the `_record_fan_state` chart tick.<br>134.3 Daily-loop seam + Climate/Tonight surfaces — `daily_loop.py` computes `overnight_away_window` alongside the existing inclusive `active_holiday_window`; `HolidayStateOut` (`routers/daily_loop.py:601`) + shared `dailyLoopHolidayStateSchema` (`schemas.ts:1066`) gain a backend-computed `awayTonight` (= end-exclusive away), mirroring how the holiday seam itself landed (Batch 105/109). Repoint the "tonight"/climate surfaces at `awayTonight`: EnvironmentPage Climate tab (`EnvironmentPage.tsx:41`), Home Tonight + Bedroom cards (`DashboardPage.tsx:696`/`:717`), the protect-sleep suppression (`homeActions.ts:92`), and Sleep's Tonight tab (`SleepPage.tsx:238`). Leave `isActive` (inclusive) driving the surfaces that describe the away night just gone — Sleep's Last-night/history tab (`SleepPage.tsx:217`) and the all-set suppression (`DashboardPage.tsx:758`, already `isRest || isActive`) — and leave the morning brief's inclusive `insideHolidayWindow` thermal-review gate untouched, so nothing keyed to "last night" flips on `end_date` morning.<br>134.4 Tests + DECISIONS #211 — pure-function boundary (`away_overnight` true at `start`, true at `end-1`, false at `end` and after; active-only identity); each scheduler job runs on `end_date` and stays dormant on `end_date-1`; `awayTonight` true `<end` / false on `end` on the payload; Climate tab live on `end_date` while the history tab stays dormant; refresh the now-required `holiday` fixtures the way Batch 109 did. Backend pytest/ruff/mypy + web + shared vitest/tsc/eslint/build + closeout smoke. | When Mark gets home on the last day of a holiday, the bedroom/climate subsystem is live *that night* — overnight fan autopilot, bedtime thermal alert, sleep-protocol nudge, and the Climate/Home-Tonight/Sleep-Tonight surfaces all resume on `end_date` — while the day stays a plan rest and the morning "last-night" reads stay dormant. | On `end_date` the fan control acts on the live room temperature instead of the holiday-dormant no-op, the evening thermal alert and sleep nudge fire, and the Climate tab + Home Tonight/Bedroom + Sleep Tonight + protect-sleep surfaces render live rather than the "resumes …" dormant placeholder; on `end_date-1` all of those stay dormant; the day's planned workout stays `skipped` and the morning brief thermal review + Sleep Last-night/history tab stay dormant on `end_date` morning; `awayTonight` is a documented shared-schema field distinct from the end-inclusive `isActive`; **no migration**; the propose→approve→push contract, Green/Amber/Red, #133, #135, and Red-never-VO2 are untouched; backend pytest/ruff/mypy and web + shared vitest/tsc/eslint/build green; closeout smoke. |
